## Culture names notes
#Cultures should eventually be batched to map to the following
#	Byzantine Cultures should use greek
#	Slavic Cultures should use old_slavic
#	German Cultures should use german
#	Celtic Cultures should use gallic

#Moved duchies
#d_ragusa moved to k_croatia to match 395 borders

#Removed WtWSMS duchies
#d_andatuonia dropped, as it is split between d_slavonia, d_bosna, d_dalmatia, and d_usora
#d_eurgegius, d_bodensee, d_noricum dropped given finer detail in k_raetia_noricum

#Moved Baronies
#Moved b_marseille from c_provence into c_venaissin to better match 395 provinces
#Moved b_annaba (Hippo Regius) from c_annaba into c_satfura to give Numida coastal access w/o splitting Hippo from d_africa_proconsularis
#Moved b_ilerena from c_badajoz to c_medellin to better capture Lusitania's presence on the east bank of the guadiana
#Moved b_mabij and b_azaz from c_aleppo to c_aintab to put the capital of d_euphratensis with d_euphratensis

#Other notes:
#c_almeria **_should_** be split so that almeria goes to d_aetica, ... but only b_almeria should go the d_baetica; 
#	c_almeria moved to d_carthaginensis instead
#c_molina should be in d_tarraconensis, but it would make d_carthaginensis split by the mountains, 
#	so moved to d_carthaginensis
#b_skopje is right on the southern border for d_dardania, so c_skopje should probably be split
#c_skopje needs to be split to better support d_macedonia_prima and d_macedonia_salutaris
#County borders make Philippopolis vs. Haemimontus bordrs very awkward/innaccurate
#Merged both phrygias for lack of space
#c_phrygia should be split so b_katyaion and b_dorylaion can be part of c_phrygia
#	also Pessinius to d_galatia_secunda_salutaris
#Should redo euphrates county borders for d_euphratensis

e_italia = {
	color={ 220 20 60 }
	color2={ 255 255 255 }
	
	capital = c_roma # Rome

		if = {
			limit = { culture = culture:italian }
			add = @correct_culture_primary_score
		}
	}
	
	can_create = {
		if = {
			limit = { is_ai = yes }
			always = no
		}
	}
